user)\npop_ct=pd.crosstab(u[u.city.isin(big)].city,u[u.city.isin(big)].user_type)\ntype_rates=pb.groupby(['user_type','category_name']).size().unstack(fill_value=0).div(u[u.city.isin(big)].user_type.value_counts(), type_rates.loc[t].reindex(obs.columns).fillna(0))\nres3=(obs-exp3)/np.sqrt(exp3)\nprint('\\\\nUser population type-rate expected negative residuals:')\nfor (city,catn),z in {"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_26","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\nimport pandas as pd, glob, numpy as np\nfrom scipy.stats import poisson\nfrom statsmodels.stats.multitest import multipletests\nu=pd.read_csv('user_001.csv')\ncat=pd.read_csv('category_001.csv')\nl=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('listing_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\ncatmap=cat.set_index('category_id').category_name\ncity_counts=u.city.value_counts(); big=city_counts[city_counts>=50].index\n# events by city/type/cat\np=pd.read_csv('purchase_001.csv').rename(columns={'buyer_id':'user_id','purchase_time':'timestamp'})[['user_id','listing_id','timestamp']].merge(l[['listing_id','category_id']],on='listing_id')\ns=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('search_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)[['user_id','category_id','timestamp']]\nimp=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('impression_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)[['user_id','listing_id','timestamp']].merge(l[['listing_id','category_id']],on='listing_id')\nclick=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('click_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)[['user_id','listing_id','timestamp']].merge(l[['listing_id','category_id']],on='listing_id')\nfav=pd.read_csv('favorite_event_001.csv')[['user_id','listing_id','timestamp']].merge(l[['listing_id','category_id']],on='listing_id')\n\ndef prep(df):\n    df=df.merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']],on='user_id')\n    df=df[df.city.isin(big)].copy()\n    df['category_name']=df.category_id.map(catmap)\n    return df\np=prep(p); s=prep(s); imp=prep(imp); click=prep(click); fav=prep(fav)\n# Aggregate counts by city,type,cat for source and purchase. Expected purchase = source city-type-cat * global type-category p/source ratio? maybe category-specific/type-specific conversion.\ndef conv(source, srcname):\n    # observed purchase city-cat\n    obs=p.groupby(['city','category_name']).size().unstack(fill_value=0)\n    source_counts=source.groupby(['city','user_type','category_name']).size()\n    # global rates per user_type, category: purchases/source (guard)\n    p_counts=p.groupby(['user_type','category_name']).size()\n    src_counts=source.groupby(['user_type','category_name']).size()\n    rates=(p_counts/src_counts).replace([np.inf,-np.inf],np.nan).fillna(0)\n    exp=pd.DataFrame(0.0,index=obs.index,columns=obs.columns)\n    for (city,t,c),n in source_counts.items():\n        if c in exp.columns and city in exp.index:\n            exp.loc[city,c]+=n*rates.get((t,c),0)\n    # If city category no source, exp=0; here all mostly\n    res=(obs-exp)/np.sqrt(exp.replace(0,np.nan))\n    ratio=obs/exp.replace(0,np.nan)\n    recs=[]\n    for city in obs.index:\n        for c in obs.columns:\n            lam=exp.loc[city,c]; k=obs.loc[city,c]\n            if lam>0:\n                recs.append((poisson.cdf(k,lam),city,c,k,lam,res.loc[city,c],ratio.loc[city,c]))\n    q=multipletests([r[0] for r in recs],alpha=0.05,method='fdr_bh')[1]\n    rows=sorted([(*r,qq) for r,qq in zip(recs,q)])\n    print('\\\\nPurchase expected from',srcname,'BH<.05',sum(r[-1]<.05 for r in rows),'q<.1',sum(r[-1]<.1 for r in rows))\n    for r in rows[:30]:\n        pval,city,c,k,lam,z,ratio,qq=r\n        print(f'p={pval:.2e} q={qq:.3g} {city:15s} {c:22s} z={z:6.2f} ratio={ratio:.2f} obs={k:3d} exp={lam:5.1f}')\nfor source,name in [(s,'search'),(imp,'impression'),(click,'click'),(fav,'favorite')]: conv(source,name)\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

lam=expP.loc[city,c]; pval=poisson.cdf(k,lam)\n        impz=metrics['impression'][2].loc[city,c]\n        clickz=metrics['click'][2].loc[city,c]\n        favz=metrics['favorite'][2].loc[city,c]\n        # rule variants\n        if pval<0.01 and ratP.loc[city,c]<0.6 and (impz<-8 or clickz<-3 or favz<-2.5):\n            selected.append((city,c,pval,resP.loc[city,c],ratP.loc[city,c],impz,clickz,favz,k,lam))\nfor r in sorted(selected):\n    city,c,pv,z,rat,impz,clickz,favz,k,lam=r\n    print(f'{city:15s} {c:22s} p={pv:.1e} pz={z:5.2f} ratio={rat:.2f} impz={impz:6.2f} clickz={clickz:5.2f} favz={favz:5.2f} obs={k:.0f} exp={lam:.1f}')\nprint('count',len(selected))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

fallback category/type\nstrata=['user_type','category_name','condition','month','price_bin']\n# compute global stratum sold/count and city stratum sold/count for leave city out\ng=m.groupby(strata).sold.agg(['sum','count'])\ng2=m.groupby(['city']+strata).sold.agg(['sum','count'])\n# fallback category+user_type+condition maybe\nfb=m.groupby(['user_type','category_name']).sold.agg(['sum','count'])\nrecs=[]\nfor (city,c),grp in m.groupby(['city','category_name']):\n    n=len(grp); k=int(grp.sold.sum())\n    if n<10: continue\n    exp=0.0\n    for _,row in grp.iterrows():\n        key=tuple(row[s] for s in strata)\n        gs=g.loc[key]\n        try:\n            cs=g2.loc[(city,)+key]\n            denom=gs['count']-cs['count']; num=gs['sum']-cs['sum']\n        except KeyError:\n            denom=gs['count']; num=gs['sum']\n        if denom>=20:\n            rate=num/denom\n        else:\n            fbkey=(row['user_type'],row['category_name'])\n            f=fb.loc[fbkey]\n            # leave current city approximate subtract city category user type\n            rate=f['sum']/f['count']\n        exp+=rate\n    # use binomial p with avg exp/n rough; z\n    p0=exp/n if n else 0\n    if p0<=0 or p0>=1: continue\n    z=(k-exp)/np.sqrt(n*p0*(1-p0))\n    pval=binomtest(k,n,p0,alternative='less').pvalue\n    recs.append((pval,city,c,k,n,exp,k/n,p0,z))\nq=multipletests([r[0] for r in recs],alpha=0.05,method='fdr_bh')[1]\nrows=sorted([(*r,qq) for r,qq in zip(recs,q)])\nprint('q<.05',sum(r[-1]<.05 for r in rows),'q<.1',sum(r[-1]<.1 for r in rows))\nfor r in rows[:60]:\n    pval,city,c,k,n,exp,rate,p0,z,qq=r\n    print(f'p={pval:.2e} q={qq:.3g} {city:15s} {c:22s} z={z:5.2f} sold={k:3d}/{n:3d} rate={rate:.2f} exp={exp:.1f} p0={p0:.2f}')\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
